### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-966">Log de stdout do módulo ASP.NET Core (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-966">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-967">O log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core geralmente registra mensagens de erro úteis não encontradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-967">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-968">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-968">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-969">Navegue até a folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** no portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-969">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-970">Em **SELECIONAR CATEGORIA DE PROBLEMA**, selecione o botão **Aplicativo Web Inoperante**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-970">Under **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY**, select the **Web App Down** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-971">Em **Soluções Sugeridas** > **Habilitar o Redirecionamento de Log de Stdout**, selecione o botão para **Abrir o Console do Kudu para editar o Web.Config**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-971">Under **Suggested Solutions** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection**, select the button to **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-972">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, abra as pastas no caminho **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-972">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-973">Role para baixo para revelar o arquivo *web.config* na parte inferior da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-973">Scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-974">Clique no ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-974">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-975">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-975">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-976">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-976">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-977">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-977">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-978">Retorne ao portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-978">Return to the Azure portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-979">Selecione a folha **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-979">Select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-980">Selecione o **botão &rarr; ir** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-980">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-981">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-981">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-982">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-982">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-983">Abra a pasta **LogFiles**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-983">Select the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-984">Inspecione a coluna **Modificado em** e selecione o ícone de lápis para editar o log de stdout com a data da última modificação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-984">Inspect the **Modified** column and select the pencil icon to edit the stdout log with the latest modification date.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-985">Quando o arquivo de log é aberto, o erro é exibido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-985">When the log file opens, the error is displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-986">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-986">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-987">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, retorne para o caminho **site** > **wwwroot** para revelar o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-987">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, return to the path **site** > **wwwroot** to reveal the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-988">Abra o arquivo **web.config** novamente, selecionando o ícone de lápis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-988">Open the **web.config** file again by selecting the pencil icon.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-989">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-989">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-990">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-990">Select **Save** to save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-991">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-991">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-992">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-992">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-993">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-993">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-994">Somente use o log de stdout para solucionar problemas de inicialização de aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-994">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-995">Para registro em log geral em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core após a inicialização, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-995">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-996">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-996">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-997">Aplicativo lento ou suspenso (serviço de Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-997">Slow or hanging app (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-998">Para saber mais sobre quando um aplicativo responde lentamente ou trava em uma solicitação, confira os seguintes artigos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-998">When an app responds slowly or hangs on a request, see the following articles:</span></span>

* [<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1000">Use a Extensão de Site do Diagnosticador de Falhas para capturar o despejo para problemas de exceção intermitentes ou problemas de desempenho no aplicativo Web do Azure</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1000">Use Crash Diagnoser Site Extension to Capture Dump for Intermittent Exception issues or performance issues on Azure Web App</span></span>](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/asiatech/2015/12/28/use-crash-diagnoser-site-extension-to-capture-dump-for-intermittent-exception-issues-or-performance-issues-on-azure-web-app/)

### <a name="monitoring-blades"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1001">Folhas de monitoramento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1001">Monitoring blades</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1002">As folhas de monitoramento fornecem uma experiência alternativa de solução de problemas para os métodos descritos anteriormente no tópico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1002">Monitoring blades provide an alternative troubleshooting experience to the methods described earlier in the topic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1003">Essas folhas podem ser usadas para diagnosticar erros da série 500.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1003">These blades can be used to diagnose 500-series errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1004">Verifique se as Extensões do ASP.NET Core estão instaladas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1004">Confirm that the ASP.NET Core Extensions are installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1005">Se as extensões não estiverem instaladas, instale-as manualmente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1005">If the extensions aren't installed, install them manually:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1006">Na seção de folha **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO**, selecione a folha **Extensões**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1006">In the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** blade section, select the **Extensions** blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1007">As **Extensões do ASP.NET Core** devem aparecer na lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1007">The **ASP.NET Core Extensions** should appear in the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1008">Se as extensões não estiverem instaladas, selecione o botão **Adicionar**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1008">If the extensions aren't installed, select the **Add** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1009">Escolha as **Extensões do ASP.NET Core** da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1009">Choose the **ASP.NET Core Extensions** from the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1010">Selecione **OK** para aceitar os termos legais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1010">Select **OK** to accept the legal terms.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1011">Selecione **OK** na folha **Adicionar extensão**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1011">Select **OK** on the **Add extension** blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1012">Uma mensagem pop-up informativa indica quando as extensões são instaladas com êxito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1012">An informational pop-up message indicates when the extensions are successfully installed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1013">Se o registro em log de stdout não estiver habilitado, siga estas etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1013">If stdout logging isn't enabled, follow these steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1014">No portal do Azure, selecione a folha **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1014">In the Azure portal, select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1015">Selecione o **botão &rarr; ir** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1015">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1016">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1016">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1017">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1017">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1018">Abra as pastas no caminho **site** > **wwwroot** e role para baixo para revelar o arquivo *web.config* na parte inferior da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1018">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot** and scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1019">Clique no ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1019">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1020">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1020">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1021">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1021">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1022">Prossiga para ativar o log de diagnóstico:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1022">Proceed to activate diagnostic logging:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1023">No portal do Azure, selecione a folha **Logs de diagnóstico**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1023">In the Azure portal, select the **Diagnostics logs** blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1024">Selecione a opção **Ligado** para **Log de Aplicativo (Sistema de arquivos)** e **Mensagens de erro detalhadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1024">Select the **On** switch for **Application Logging (Filesystem)** and **Detailed error messages**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1025">Selecione o botão **Salvar** na parte superior da folha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1025">Select the **Save** button at the top of the blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1026">Para incluir o rastreamento de solicitação com falha, também conhecido como FREB (Buffer de Evento de Solicitação com Falha), selecione a opção **Ligado** para o **Rastreamento de solicitação com falha**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1026">To include failed request tracing, also known as Failed Request Event Buffering (FREB) logging, select the **On** switch for **Failed request tracing**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1027">Selecione a folha **Fluxo de log**, que é listada imediatamente sob a folha **Logs de diagnóstico** no portal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1027">Select the **Log stream** blade, which is listed immediately under the **Diagnostics logs** blade in the portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1028">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1028">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1029">Dentro dos dados de fluxo de log, a causa do erro é indicada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1029">Within the log stream data, the cause of the error is indicated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1030">Sempre desabilite o registro em log de stdout após concluir a solução de problemas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1030">Be sure to disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1031">Para exibir os logs de rastreamento de solicitação com falha (logs FREB):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1031">To view the failed request tracing logs (FREB logs):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1032">Navegue até a folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** no portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1032">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1033">Selecione **Logs de Rastreamento de Solicitação com Falha** da área **FERRAMENTAS DE SUPORTE** da barra lateral.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1033">Select **Failed Request Tracing Logs** from the **SUPPORT TOOLS** area of the sidebar.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1034">Confira a [seção de Rastreamentos de solicitação com falha no tópico Habilitar o log de diagnósticos para aplicativos Web no Serviço de Aplicativo do Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) e as [Perguntas frequentes do desempenho do aplicativo para Aplicativos Web no Azure: como ativar o rastreamento de solicitação com falha?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) para obter mais informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1034">See [Failed request traces section of the Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service topic](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) and the [Application performance FAQs for Web Apps in Azure: How do I turn on failed request tracing?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) for more information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1035">Para obter mais informações, veja [Habilitar log de diagnósticos para aplicativos Web no Serviço de Aplicativo do Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1035">For more information, see [Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1036">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1036">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1037">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1037">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1038">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1038">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1039">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1039">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1040">Solução de problemas no IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1040">Troubleshoot on IIS</span></span>

### <a name="application-event-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1041">Log de eventos do aplicativo (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1041">Application Event Log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1042">Acesse o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1042">Access the Application Event Log:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1043">Abra o menu Iniciar, procure *Visualizador de eventos* e selecione o aplicativo **Visualizador de eventos** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1043">Open the Start menu, search for *Event Viewer*, and select the **Event Viewer** app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1044">No **Visualizador de Eventos**, abra o nó **Logs do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1044">In **Event Viewer**, open the **Windows Logs** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1045">Selecione **Aplicativo** para abrir o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1045">Select **Application** to open the Application Event Log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1046">Procure erros associados ao aplicativo com falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1046">Search for errors associated with the failing app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1047">Os erros têm um valor *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS* ou *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS Express* na coluna *Origem*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1047">Errors have a value of *IIS AspNetCore Module* or *IIS Express AspNetCore Module* in the *Source* column.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-at-a-command-prompt"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1048">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1048">Run the app at a command prompt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1049">Muitos erros de inicialização não produzem informações úteis no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1049">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1050">Você pode encontrar a causa de alguns erros ao executar o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1050">You can find the cause of some errors by running the app at a command prompt on the hosting system.</span></span>

#### <a name="framework-dependent-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1051">Implantação dependente de estrutura</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1051">Framework-dependent deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1052">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1052">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1053">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o aplicativo, executando o assembly do aplicativo com *dotnet.exe*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1053">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app by executing the app's assembly with *dotnet.exe*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1054">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name> : `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1054">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1055">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1055">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1056">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1056">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1057">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1057">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1058">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1058">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

#### <a name="self-contained-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1059">Implantação autocontida</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1059">Self-contained deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1060">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1060">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1061">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o arquivo executável do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1061">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app's executable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1062">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name> : `<assembly_name>.exe` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1062">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `<assembly_name>.exe`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1063">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1063">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1064">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1064">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1065">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1065">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1066">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1066">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1067">Log de stdout do módulo ASP.NET Core (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1067">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1068">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1068">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1069">Navegue até a pasta de implantação do site no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1069">Navigate to the site's deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1070">Se a pasta *logs* não estiver presente, crie-a.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1070">If the *logs* folder isn't present, create the folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1071">Para obter instruções sobre como habilitar o MSBuild para criar a pasta *logs* na implantação automaticamente, veja o tópico [Estrutura de diretórios](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1071">For instructions on how to enable MSBuild to create the *logs* folder in the deployment automatically, see the [Directory structure](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure) topic.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1072">Edite o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1072">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1073">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para apontar para a pasta *logs* (por exemplo, `.\logs\stdout`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1073">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to point to the *logs* folder (for example, `.\logs\stdout`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1074">`stdout` no caminho é o prefixo do nome do arquivo de log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1074">`stdout` in the path is the log file name prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1075">Uma extensão de arquivo, uma ID do processo e um carimbo de data/hora são adicionados automaticamente quando o log é criado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1075">A timestamp, process id, and file extension are added automatically when the log is created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1076">Usando `stdout` como o prefixo do nome do arquivo, um arquivo de log típico é nomeado *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1076">Using `stdout` as the file name prefix, a typical log file is named *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1077">Verifique se a identidade do pool de aplicativos tem permissões de gravação para a pasta *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1077">Ensure your application pool's identity has write permissions to the *logs* folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1078">Salve o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1078">Save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1079">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1079">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1080">Navegue até a pasta *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1080">Navigate to the *logs* folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1081">Localize e abra o log de stdout mais recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1081">Find and open the most recent stdout log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1082">Estude o log em busca de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1082">Study the log for errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1083">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1083">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1084">Edite o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1084">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1085">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1085">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1086">Salve o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1086">Save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1087">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1087">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1088">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1088">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1089">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1089">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1090">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1090">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1091">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1091">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-developer-exception-page"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1092">Habilitar a página de exceção do desenvolvedor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1092">Enable the Developer Exception Page</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1093">A  [variável de ambiente `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` pode ser adicionada ao web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) para executar o aplicativo no ambiente de desenvolvimento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1093">The `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` [environment variable can be added to web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) to run the app in the Development environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1094">Desde que o ambiente não seja substituído na inicialização do aplicativo por `UseEnvironment` no compilador do host, definir a variável de ambiente permite que a [Página de Exceções do Desenvolvedor](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) apareça quando o aplicativo é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1094">As long as the environment isn't overridden in app startup by `UseEnvironment` on the host builder, setting the environment variable allows the [Developer Exception Page](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) to appear when the app is run.</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore processPath="dotnet"
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll"
      stdoutLogEnabled="false"
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout">
  <environmentVariables>
    <environmentVariable name="ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT" value="Development" />
  </environmentVariables>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1095">Configurar a variável de ambiente para `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` só é recomendado para servidores de preparo e de teste que não estejam expostos à Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1095">Setting the environment variable for `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` is only recommended for use on staging and testing servers that aren't exposed to the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1096">Remova a variável de ambiente do arquivo *web.config* após a solução de problemas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1096">Remove the environment variable from the *web.config* file after troubleshooting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1097">Para obter informações sobre como definir variáveis de ambiente no *web.config*, confira [Elemento filho environmentVariables de aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1097">For information on setting environment variables in *web.config*, see [environmentVariables child element of aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span></span>

### <a name="obtain-data-from-an-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1098">Obter dados de um aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1098">Obtain data from an app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1099">Se um aplicativo for capaz de responder às solicitações, obtenha as solicitações, conexão e dados adicionais do aplicativo que usar o middleware embutido de terminal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1099">If an app is capable of responding to requests, obtain request, connection, and additional data from the app using terminal inline middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1100">Para saber mais e obter um código de exemplo, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1100">For more information and sample code, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1101">Aplicativo lento ou suspenso (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1101">Slow or hanging app (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1102">Um *despejo* é um instantâneo da memória do sistema e pode ajudar a determinar a causa de uma falha de aplicativo, de inicialização ou de um aplicativo lento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1102">A *crash dump* is a snapshot of the system's memory and can help determine the cause of an app crash, startup failure, or slow app.</span></span>

#### <a name="app-crashes-or-encounters-an-exception"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1103">O aplicativo falha ou encontra uma exceção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1103">App crashes or encounters an exception</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1104">Obter e analisar um despejo de memória do [WER (Relatório de Erros do Windows)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1104">Obtain and analyze a dump from [Windows Error Reporting (WER)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1105">Crie uma pasta para armazenar os arquivos de despejo de memória em `c:\dumps`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1105">Create a folder to hold crash dump files at `c:\dumps`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1106">O pool de aplicativos deve ter acesso para gravação à pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1106">The app pool must have write access to the folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1107">Execute o [script EnableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1107">Run the [EnableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1108">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1108">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps w3wp.exe c:\dumps
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1109">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1109">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps dotnet.exe c:\dumps
     ```

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1110">Execute o aplicativo sob as condições que causam a falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1110">Run the app under the conditions that cause the crash to occur.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1111">Após a falha, execute o [script DisableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1111">After the crash has occurred, run the [DisableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1112">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1112">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps w3wp.exe
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1113">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1113">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps dotnet.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1114">Depois que um aplicativo falhar e a coleta de despejo de memória for concluída, o aplicativo terá permissão para encerrar normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1114">After an app crashes and dump collection is complete, the app is allowed to terminate normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1115">O script do PowerShell configura o WER para coletar até cinco despejos de memória por aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1115">The PowerShell script configures WER to collect up to five dumps per app.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1116">Os despejos de memória podem usar uma grande quantidade de espaço em disco (até vários gigabytes cada).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1116">Crash dumps might take up a large amount of disk space (up to several gigabytes each).</span></span>

#### <a name="app-hangs-fails-during-startup-or-runs-normally"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1117">O aplicativo trava, falha durante a inicialização ou executa normalmente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1117">App hangs, fails during startup, or runs normally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1118">Quando um aplicativo *paralisa* (para de responder, mas não falha), falha durante a inicialização ou é executado normalmente, consulte [arquivos de despejo no modo de usuário: escolhendo a melhor ferramenta](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) para selecionar uma ferramenta apropriada para produzir o despejo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1118">When an app *hangs* (stops responding but doesn't crash), fails during startup, or runs normally, see [User-Mode Dump Files: Choosing the Best Tool](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) to select an appropriate tool to produce the dump.</span></span>

#### <a name="analyze-the-dump"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1119">Analisar o despejo de memória</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1119">Analyze the dump</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1120">Um despejo de memória pode ser analisado usando várias abordagens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1120">A dump can be analyzed using several approaches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1121">Para obter mais informações, confira [Analisando um arquivo de despejo de memória do modo de usuário](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1121">For more information, see [Analyzing a User-Mode Dump File](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span></span>

## <a name="clear-package-caches"></a><span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1122">Limpar caches de pacote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1122">Clear package caches</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1123">Um aplicativo em funcionamento pode falhar imediatamente após a atualização do SDK do .NET Core no computador de desenvolvimento ou a alteração das versões do pacote no aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1123">A functioning app may fail immediately after upgrading either the .NET Core SDK on the development machine or changing package versions within the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1124">Em alguns casos, pacotes incoerentes podem interromper um aplicativo ao executar atualizações principais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1124">In some cases, incoherent packages may break an app when performing major upgrades.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1125">A maioria desses problemas pode ser corrigida seguindo estas instruções:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1125">Most of these issues can be fixed by following these instructions:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1126">Exclua as pastas *bin* e *obj*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1126">Delete the *bin* and *obj* folders.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1127">Limpe os caches de pacote executando [dotnet NuGet local All--Clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) de um shell de comando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1127">Clear the package caches by executing [dotnet nuget locals all --clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) from a command shell.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1128">Limpar caches de pacote também pode ser feito com a ferramenta de [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) e executar o comando `nuget locals all -clear` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1128">Clearing package caches can also be accomplished with the [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) tool and executing the command `nuget locals all -clear`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1129">*nuget.exe* não é uma instalação fornecida com o sistema operacional Windows Desktop e devem ser obtidos separadamente do [site do NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1129">*nuget.exe* isn't a bundled install with the Windows desktop operating system and must be obtained separately from the [NuGet website](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1130">Restaure e recompile o projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1130">Restore and rebuild the project.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b31cd-1131">Exclua todos os arquivos na pasta de implantação no servidor antes de reimplantar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b31cd-1131">Delete all of the files in the deployment folder on the server prior to redeploying the app.</span></span>
